		<article id="post-28250" class="post-28250 recipe type-recipe status-publish has-post-thumbnail hentry recipe_category-appetizers recipe_category-thanksgiving recipe_category-holiday-dishes">

				<header class="section-introduction ">
					<h1 class="entry-title">Gluten-Free Brie Bites</h1>
					<a href="#wprm-recipe-container-28293" data-recipe="28293" style="color: #333333;" class="wprm-recipe-jump wprm-recipe-link wprm-jump-to-recipe-shortcode wprm-block-text-normal">Jump to Recipe</a>					<p class="post-date">Published on December 13, 2023</p>					<!--<p class="post-modified-info">Last Updated on December 14, 2025</p>-->
					<p class="subtitle">A gluten-free puff pastry appetizer everyone will rave about! Just 4 ingredients, it's gluten-free puff pastry filled with brie and either cranberry sauce or fig jam, then baked to golden, melty perfection. Super easy recipe can be prepped ahead.</p>

					<h3 class="recipe-caption">Easy recipe for Gluten-Free Brie Bites Appetizer!</h3>					
					</div>
				<div class="wprm-recipe wprm-recipe-snippet wprm-recipe-template-hgff-2"><a href="#recipe" data-recipe="28293" style="color: #ffffff;background-color: #7bb664;border-color: #7bb664;border-radius: 5px;padding: 5px 5px;" class="wprm-recipe-jump wprm-recipe-link wprm-jump-to-recipe-shortcode wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-jump-inline-button wprm-recipe-link-inline-button wprm-color-accent">Jump to Recipe</a></div>					<div class="recipe-introduction">

						<p>For <a href="https://www.healthygffamily.com/recipe/mediterranean-vegetarian-stuffed-mushrooms/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mediterranean Stuffed Mushrooms, </a><a href="https://www.healthygffamily.com/recipe/sweet-spicy-mixed-nuts/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Sweet &amp; Spicy Mixed Nuts,</a> <a href="https://www.healthygffamily.com/recipe/baked-brie-with-cranberry-chutney-gluten-free/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Baked Brie with Cranberry Chutney,</a> <a href="https://www.healthygffamily.com/recipe/mini-spinach-pies/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Spinach Pie Bites</a>, <a href="https://www.healthygffamily.com/recipe/spinach-artichoke-dip/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">a healthier Spinach Artichoke Dip</a>, and more <a href="https://www.healthygffamily.com/recipe_category/appetizers/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">holiday appetizers.</a></p>
<p>Just in time for the holidays, sharing these <em>Gluten-Free Brie Bites!</em></p>
<p>They are <strong>a gluten-free puff pastry appetizer everyone will rave about!</strong></p>
<p>It is a gluten-free puff pastry filled with brie, either cranberry sauce or fig jam and a sprinkling of pecans (optional but adds great crunch), then baked to golden, melty perfection&#8230; and they are so delicious!</p>
<p>The<strong> brie is warm and melty</strong>, and whether you top it with <strong>tart cranberry sauce or slightly sweeter fig jam</strong>, each bite <strong>paired with golden, buttery gluten-free puff pastry</strong> <strong>is divine!</strong></p>
<p><strong>Top with a sprig of fresh rosemary for a festive pop of color and they are a show stopper!</strong></p>
<p>And the easy <strong>4</strong> <strong>ingredient recipe comes together in no time!</strong></p>

<h3>How to Make Gluten-Free Brie Bites</h3>
<p>There are lots of recipes for similar bites, I adapted this one from <a href="https://www.wellplated.com/brie-bites/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Well Plated by Erin.</a></p>
<p><strong>Here are the ingredients you&#8217;ll need:</strong></p>
<p><em>gluten-free puff pastry</em> (We used Schar Puff Pastry. This recipe is the first time we&#8217;ve used Schar Puff Pastry and we loved it! Easy to work with and bakes up to golden puff pastry with great flavor, and it holds together well once baked).</p>
<p><em>brie cheese</em></p>
<p><em>cranberry sauce*</em> (we used our <a href="https://www.healthygffamily.com/recipe/famous-cranberry-sauce/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Famous Cranberry Sauce</a>)</p>
<p><em>*or  fig jam</em></p>
<p><em>finely chopped pecans</em></p>
<p><em>fresh rosemary</em> (optional but adds a nice festive pop of color)</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="lazy lazy-hidden aligncenter wp-image-28256" src="//www.healthygffamily.com/wp-content/plugins/a3-lazy-load/assets/images/lazy_placeholder.gif" data-lazy-type="image" <h3>Step by Step How to Make Gluten-Free Brie Bites</h3>
<p>They take about<strong> 15 minutes to prepare</strong> and come together in just a few simple steps.</p>
<p><strong>The first thing to do is make the gluten-free puff pastry cups:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Thaw the gluten-free puff pastry according to the package. Roll flat and slice into 16 squares (approximately 2 1/2 inches each)</li>
<li>Press each square into a well oiled mini muffin tin. This will create your gluten-free puff pastry cup. They won&#8217;t all look the same and that&#8217;s perfectly fine!</li>
</ul>

https://www.healthygffamily.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/2B7CFD35-3CE4-4FA3-AFC2-660DBF53D15A-1536x2048.jpg 1536w, https://www.healthygffamily.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/2B7CFD35-3CE4-4FA3-AFC2-660DBF53D15A-540x720.jpg 540w, https://www.healthygffamily.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/2B7CFD35-3CE4-4FA3-AFC2-660DBF53D15A-640x853.jpg 640w, https://www.healthygffamily.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/12/2B7CFD35-3CE4-4FA3-AFC2-660DBF53D15A-150x200.jpg 150w" sizes="(max-width: 1920px) 100vw, 1920px" /></noscript></a>
			</div></figure><figure class='gallery-item'>
			<div class='gallery-icon portrait'>
				<a href='https://www.healthygffamily.com/recipe/gluten-free-brie-bites-appetizer/attachment/618fb226-68dd-4837-8f66-90ff119b3e0a/'><img width="1915" height="2560" 			</div></figure>
		</div>

<p><strong>Slice the brie</strong> into 1/2 -3/4 inch pieces.  Tips: refrigerate until ready to slice so that it slices easier and use a sharp knife or cheese slicer.</p>
<p><strong>Place each piece of brie into the gluten-free pasty cup.</strong></p>
<p><strong>Top with either cranberry sauce or fig jam</strong>. <strong>The cranberry sauc</strong>e looks festive with the pop of red and has nice tart contrast with the nutty buttery brie. <strong>The fig jam</strong> is slightly sweeter, but fig jam and brie is one of my favorite combinations so you can&#8217;t go wrong with either.  <strong>You could also try a raspberry jam</strong> if you want the red color and a slightly tarter jam.</p>
<p><strong>Top with a sprinkle of chopped pecans</strong> if you&#8217;re not nut-free. They add a nice crunchy contrast to the melty brie and puff pastry.</p>

		</div>

<p>And bake!</p>
<p>They bake until the gluten-free puff pastry is golden and the brie is melty. If any of the brie or jam comes out of the puff pastry, just spoon it back in, no one will notice.</p>
<p>Remove from the oven and let sit just 3-5 minutes, then using a fork transfer from the muffin tins to a serving plate and top a few with a spring of rosemary.</p>

<p>They can be served warm or room temperature.</p>
<p>And whether you opt for the cranberry sauce or fig jam, they are both so delicious with the contrasts of flavors and textures.</p>

<h3>Storing and Making Ahead</h3>
<p><strong>To make ahead you could either:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li>Bake them and then reheat in the oven or microwave.</li>
<li>Or prepare them up to baking, cover loosely with wax paper and refrigerate, then bring room temperature and bake when ready to serve.</li>
</ol>
<p>I prefer the second option when first serving them to friends and family. But leftovers reheat well!</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name wprm-block-text-bold">Gluten-Free Brie Bites</h2>
<div class="wprm-spacer" style="height: 5px;"></div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary wprm-block-text-normal"><span style="display: block;">A gluten-free puff pastry appetizer everyone will rave about! Just 4 ingredients, it&#039;s gluten-free puff pastry filled with brie and either cranberry sauce or fig jam, then baked to golden, melty perfection. Super easy recipe can be prepped ahead.</span></div>
<div class="wprm-spacer"></div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-meta-container wprm-recipe-times-container wprm-recipe-details-container wprm-recipe-details-container-table wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-table-borders-top-bottom wprm-recipe-table-borders-inside" style="border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: #777777;"><div class="wprm-recipe-block-container wprm-recipe-block-container-table wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-time-container wprm-recipe-prep-time-container" style="border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: #777777;"><span class="wprm-recipe-details-label wprm-block-text-faded wprm-recipe-time-label wprm-recipe-prep-time-label">Prep Time</span><span class="wprm-recipe-time wprm-block-text-normal"><span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time wprm-recipe-prep_time-minutes">15<span class="sr-only screen-reader-text wprm-screen-reader-text"> minutes</span></span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details-unit wprm-recipe-details-minutes wprm-recipe-prep_time-unit wprm-recipe-prep_timeunit-minutes" aria-hidden="true">mins</span></span></div></div>
<div class="wprm-spacer" style="height: 5px;"></div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-meta-container wprm-recipe-tags-container wprm-recipe-details-container wprm-recipe-details-container-inline wprm-block-text-normal"><div class="wprm-recipe-block-container wprm-recipe-block-container-inline wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-tag-container wprm-recipe-course-container" style=""><span class="wprm-recipe-details-label wprm-block-text-faded wprm-recipe-tag-label wprm-recipe-course-label">Course: </span><span class="wprm-recipe-course wprm-block-text-normal">Appetizer, Holidays</span></div><div class="wprm-recipe-block-container wprm-recipe-block-container-inline wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-tag-container wprm-recipe-cuisine-container" style=""><span class="wprm-recipe-details-label wprm-block-text-faded wprm-recipe-tag-label wprm-recipe-cuisine-label">Cuisine: </span><span class="wprm-recipe-cuisine wprm-block-text-normal">Gluten-Free, Nut-Free optional</span></div><div class="wprm-recipe-block-container wprm-recipe-block-container-inline wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-tag-container wprm-recipe-keyword-container" style=""><span class="wprm-recipe-details-label wprm-block-text-faded wprm-recipe-tag-label wprm-recipe-keyword-label">Keyword: </span><span class="wprm-recipe-keyword wprm-block-text-normal">easy gluten-free appetizer, gluten-free holiday appetizer, gluten-free brie bites, gluten-free puff pastry appetizer</span></div></div>

<div class="wprm-recipe-block-container wprm-recipe-block-container-inline wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-author-container" style=""><span class="wprm-recipe-details-label wprm-block-text-faded wprm-recipe-author-label">Author: </span><span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author wprm-block-text-normal">Healthy Gluten-free Family</span></div>

<div id="recipe-28293-equipment" class="wprm-recipe-equipment-container wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe="28293"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-equipment-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Equipment</h3><ul class="wprm-recipe-equipment wprm-recipe-equipment-list"><li class="wprm-recipe-equipment-item" style="list-style-type: disc;"><div class="wprm-recipe-equipment-name">1 24 cup mini muffin pan</div></li></ul></div>
<div id="recipe-28293-ingredients" class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container wprm-recipe-ingredients-no-images wprm-recipe-28293-ingredients-container wprm-block-text-normal wprm-ingredient-style-regular wprm-recipe-images-before" data-recipe="28293" data-servings="24"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-ingredients-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Ingredients</h3><div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group"><ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients"><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="0"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1 1/2</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">sheets </span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">gluten-free puff pastry dough</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded">we used Schar gluten-free puff pastry dough (1 box)</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="1"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">8</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">oz</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">brie cheese</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="2"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">cranberry sauce ** </span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded">we used our <a href="https://www.healthygffamily.com/recipe/famous-cranberry-sauce/">Famous Cranberry Sauce</a></span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="3"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">** OR fig jam (or a combination of the two)</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="4"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">finely chopped pecans (skip is nut-free)</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="6"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">kosher salt</span></li><li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient" style="list-style-type: disc;" data-uid="5"><span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">rosemary sprigs, cut into small pieces for serving</span>&#32;<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes-faded">optional</span></li></ul></div></div>
<div id="recipe-28293-instructions" class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-recipe-28293-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe="28293"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-none" style="">Instructions</h3><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group"><ul class="wprm-recipe-instructions"><li id="wprm-recipe-28293-step-0-0" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;">Preheat oven to 375 degrees F and generously coat muffin tins with spray oil.  </span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-28293-step-0-1" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;"><u>Puff Pastry:</u> follow the instructions on your puff pastry brand for thawing and unroll one pastry sheet at a time, and gently roll flat (the Schar pastry was quite easy to work with). Cut into 4 even lengthwise strips, then 4 even crosswise strips so that you have 16, approximately 2 1/2 inch, squares. </span><div class="wprm-spacer"></div><span style="display: block;">Press each square into the prepared muffin tin. This will create your puff pastry cup.  Repeat with the second pastry sheet but you will only use half of it and need 8 more squares/pastry cups to fill the entire 24 cup mini muffin tin.</span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-28293-step-0-2" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;"><u>Brie:</u> Refrigerate the brie until ready to cut so that it slices easily. Using a sharp knife or cheese cutting knife, slice brie into 24 1/2 - 3/4 inch pieces. Place one piece of brie in each pastry cup.</span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-28293-step-0-3" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;"><u>Top with cranberry sauce or fig jam:</u> Top with approximately 1/2 teaspoon  cranberry sauce or fig jam. They are both great tasting, so we like to do a combination.  Sprinkle with a pinch of kosher salt, then with a few chopped pecans (approximately 1/4 teaspoon), and bake for 15-18 minutes, or until pasty is golden and brie is melted.</span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-28293-step-0-4" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;">Remove from oven and let rest for a 3 minutes. If any of the brie, cranberry sauce or jam have bubbled out, just spoon it back in (no one will know!). Using a fork, carefully lift the bites out of the baking tins and onto a serving plate.  Top a few of them with rosemary sprigs to look festive and enjoy warm or room temperature.</span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-28293-step-0-5" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;">Store in the refrigerator in a sealed container and reheat in the microwave or oven.  </span></div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-28293-step-0-6" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><span style="display: block;">To make ahead, either bake fully and reheat in the oven. Or to be freshest, prepare up to the point of baking, cover gently with wax paper and refrigerate, then bring to room temperature and bake when ready to serve. Enjoy!</span></div></li></ul></div></div>

Am I the only one who had trouble with this dough? It completely cracked in multiple places when I was unrolling it. I spent more time trying to piece the dough back together and then trying to get it in to the tins without breaking apart again. I did half with fig jam and pecans, and the other half with a Pear/Honey jam and both were delicious.</p>
